 4 ibertu istory cumulative index 1953 1977 14 homesteader by frank sc wok cumulative index alberta history and its predecessor
 alberta historical review 1953 to 1977 issn 0316 1552 hi stor i cal s oc i ety o f a
 lberta box 4035 station c calgary a lberta t 2 t 5 m 9 1981 issn 03 16 1552 foreword
 when the first issue of the alberta historical review appeared in april 1953 the editor the rev w everard edmonds
 wrote that for years the society s effort to arouse general interest in its aims has been thwarted in the
 matter of publication now at last through the courtesy and co operation of the provincial government this handicap has been
 overcome this co operation which has continued over the years is further manifested in the index to the contents of
 the first 25 volumes of alberta histori as the journal has been known since the beginning of 1975 members of
 the society have long felt the need for such an index but the objective could not be realized until a
 generous grant was received in 1980 from the alberta 75 th anniversary commission we are indebted to the commission for
 its support and to joseph rek a graduate of the university of alberta s school of library science for preparing
 the index for 1953 1977 we hope that all members of the historical society of alberta and all readers of
 alberta histori will find this index a practical help in retrieving the immense amount of data tucked away in its
 pages alan d ridge two cree indians in camp near edmonton posed for photographer c w mathers in the late
